 Learn - Things related to Ashfaq Ulla Khan
 
 
 ashfak ulla khan kaa janm 22 oktober 1900 main uttar pradesh main shahjahanpur jile ke 'shahidgarh' main hua tha
 The father belonged to a Pathan family
 parivaar ke sabhi log sarkari naukari main the, lekin ashfak bachapan se hi desh ke liye kuch karnaa tha
 Let the revolutionaries of Bengal have a great influence on their lives
 swatantraaa senaanee hone ke saath kavita bhi likhte the, unhen ghudsawaari, nishanebaaji or tairaaki kaa bhi shauk tha
 Did not think that Ashfaq Ulla Khan's mind was not used to reading and writing because of his interest in reading and writing
 unhen tairaaki karnaa, bandook lekar shikaar par jane main zyada majaa aata tha
 It was true that he did not show his interest in reading and writing, but he read with great interest in the stories / stories of the movements being done for the good of the country 
 unhone kaaphi acchhee kavitaayen likhin
 In which he used to write his surname Hasrat in the poem
 vah apane liye kavita likhte the
 He had no attempt to get his poems published
 unki likhi hui kavitaayen adaalat aate-jate samay aksar 'kakori cond' ke krantikari gaaya karte the
 Kakori scandal: Such was the loot of the official treasury that the impact of Mahatma Gandhi was on Ashfaq Ullah Khan's life from the very beginning, Gandhiji withdrew the 'non-cooperation Movement' and his heart ached
 jiske baad ramprasad bismil or chandrasekhar aaazaad ke netritv main 8 agast, 1925 ko krantikariyon kii ek ahm baithak hui, jisamen 9 agast, 1925 ko saharanpur-lakhanu paisanger train kakori stesan par aane vaali train ko luutane kii yojana banaai gai jisamen sarkari khajaana tha
 The money that the revolutionaries wanted to loot, was actually the money that the British had grabbed from the Indians
 9 agast, 1925 ko ashfak ulla khan, ramprasad bismil, chandrasekhar azaad, rajendranath lahidi, thakur roshan singh, sachindra bakshi, keshav chakravarti, banavaari laal, mukunda laal or manmatha laal gupt ne apni yojana ko anjaam dete hue lakhanu ke najadik 'kakori' main train se le jaae ja rahe sarkari khajaane ko lut liya

 pataa chal gaya ki inke mansoobey kitne napak the

 vah sharia kanoon ke jariye gunahagaaron ko sajaa dena chahta he

 bagdadi ke gurgon ne bharat main havers kii fouj taiyaar karke khufia suchanaaen jutaney ke baad hamale karne kii planning kii he

 internet ke jariye jari he jangatankwaadi barood se las ISIS kii ye jang internet ke jariye anjaam tak pahunchaai ja rahi he

 baatcheet badhate hi skip ke jariye baat karte hai

 jaraa sa bhi sandigdh maaloom hone par fouran contact karte hai

 uske bare main charchaa karke soochna hasil karne kii koshish karte hai

 In the hit and run case today, superstar Salman Khan had a hearing in the sessions court of Mumbai, due to which Salman reached the court
 court main maujuud sarkari vakil ne salmaan ke driver ashok singh ke bayaan par sawaal uthaae

 lekin salmaan ne kabhi nahin use kaha kii tum police, court yaa media main jaakar sach bataao

 iske ulat salmaan ke parivaar se dryver ashol ko pyaar mil rahaa tha yah jaanate hue kii isaki karatuuton kii sajaa unke parivaar kaa ladkaa bhugat rahaa he

 kya aise gavaah par yakin kiya ja saktaa he

 darasal, biemasi ne ek aadesh jari kar kaha ki hamanen shahar main aisi 23 jagahon ko chinhit kiya he, jahaan log gaiyr-kanoonee tarise se parking karaayaa jaataa he or log be-tarateeb tareeke se apni gaadiyaan khadi karte hai
